class="ajax__tab_panel" style="visibility: visible;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures_ProductFeatureDesc">18" Barrel Stainless Steel Finish Straight Flutes Muzzle Threaded 1/2-28 Right Hand Threads 10rd<p> Our .17 HMR rifle features a standard 18" stainless steel, button-rifled 1:10 twist barrel with straight flutes, muzzle threaded 1/2-28 TPI RH for standard .223/5.56 muzzle devices, with a six vent A1 flash hider included. The weapon features a blowback operating system. The standard trigger is a military-style AR-15 trigger. Standard handguard is our G10 composite, non-vented, mid-length, free-floating tube. Standard butt stock is the M4-style, six-position, adjustable stock. The rifle ships in a soft carry bag with two 10-round magazines. Weight of rifle is 7.5 pounds. </p><p><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/darin_picures/Alexander_Arms/alex17hmr2.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="325"><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/darin_picures/Alexander_Arms/alex17hmr3.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="121"></p></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications_ProductsSpecifications"><ul><li>Barrel Length : 18</li><li>Caliber : .17 HMR</li><li>Capacity : 10</li><li>Item Description : ALX 17HMR 18 FLTD SS THRD 10</li><li>Tactica : Tactical</li><li>Threaded Barrels : Threaded Barrel</li><li>Caliber-Gauge : .17 HMR</li></ul></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Reviews"> <div id="Review"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_UpdatePnlProductReviewDetails"> <div class="Sorting"> <span class="TitleStyle"> Reviewed by <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_CustomersCnt">1</span> customer </span>&nbsp;
